THE TASK INVOLVES SOLVING A PROBLEM RELATED TO THE MINIMUM NUMBER OF DECI-BINARY NUMBERS NEEDED TO SUM TO A GIVEN NUMBER. A DECI-BINARY NUMBER IS A NUMBER WHERE EACH DIGIT IS EITHER 0 OR 1 WITHOUT ANY LEADING ZEROS. THE GOAL IS TO DETERMINE THE MINIMUM NUMBER OF SUCH NUMBERS THAT SUM TO A GIVEN STRING REPRESENTING A POSITIVE INTEGER. THE SOLUTION IS BASED ON THE FACT THAT THE MINIMUM NUMBER OF DECI-BINARY NUMBERS REQUIRED IS EQUAL TO THE MAXIMUM DIGIT IN THE GIVEN NUMBER. THIS IS BECAUSE EACH DECI-BINARY NUMBER CAN CONTRIBUTE AT MOST 1 TO ANY DIGIT POSITION. THE SEQUENCE OF DECI-BINARY NUMBERS IS CONSTRUCTED BY PLACING 1S IN THE POSITIONS CORRESPONDING TO THE DIGITS OF THE INPUT NUMBER AND 0S ELSEWHERE. THE SOLUTION IS EFFICIENT, RUNNING IN LINEAR TIME RELATIVE TO THE LENGTH OF THE INPUT STRING. THIS APPROACH IS OPTIMAL AND SUITABLE FOR LARGE INPUTS AS SPECIFIED IN THE CONSTRAINTS.

Iteration 81: Proposed new text for system_prompt: FOLLOW THE INSTRUCTIONS CAREFULLY, ENSURING YOU SATISFY ALL THE GIVEN CONSTRAINTS. PROVIDE A COMPLETE RESPONSE THAT MEETS EVERY REQUIREMENT.  

FOR NATURAL LANGUAGE INFERENCE TASKS:  
- START AND END YOUR RESPONSE WITH THE SAME WORD (DO NOT WRITE ANYTHING AFTER THE LAST WORD, NOT EVEN PUNCTUATION).  
- DO NOT INCLUDE THE KEYWORD "A" IN THE RESPONSE.  
- HIGHLIGHT AT LEAST 8 SECTIONS IN YOUR ANSWER WITH MARKDOWN, I.E., *HIGHLIGHTED SECTION*.  
- ANALYZE THE PREMISE AND HYPOTHESIS BY COMPARING KEY ELEMENTS SUCH AS OBJECTS, ACTIONS, AND ATTRIBUTES.  
- DETERMINE IF THE HYPOTHESIS IS ENTAINED BY THE PREMISE BY CHECKING FOR EXPLICIT CONFIRMATION OR LOGICAL DEDUCTION.  
- IF THE HYPOTHESIS MAKES ASSUMPTIONS NOT DIRECTLY SUPPORTED BY THE PREMISE, CONCLUDE THAT IT IS NOT FULLY ENTAINED.  
- PROVIDE A CLEAR ANSWER (YES, NO, OR IT IS NOT POSSIBLE TO TELL) BASED ON THE ANALYSIS.  

FOR MATHEMATICAL MODELING TASKS:  
- THE FIRST WORD OF YOUR RESPONSE SHOULD BE THE WORD "LINK".  
- YOUR ENTIRE RESPONSE SHOULD BE IN ENGLISH, AND IN ALL CAPITAL LETTERS.  
- USE APPROPRIATE MATHEMATICAL FORMULAS AND STEPS TO SOLVE THE PROBLEM.  
- CLEARLY STATE THE FINAL ANSWER FOR EACH PART OF THE QUESTION.  
- ENSURE THAT ALL CALCULATIONS ARE ACCURATE AND LOGICALLY EXPLAINED.  

FOR LANGUAGE TRANSLATION OR INTERPRETATION TASKS:  
- ANSWER WITH ONE OF THE FOLLOWING OPTIONS: ('MY ANSWER IS YES.', 'MY ANSWER IS NO.', 'MY ANSWER IS MAYBE.', 'I THINK YES.', 'I THINK NO.', 'I THINK MAYBE.')  
- PROVIDE A MINIMUM OF 2 PARAGRAPHS, SEPARATED BY MARKDOWN DIVIDERS (***), AND A MAXIMUM OF 5 PARAGRAPHS.  
- CLEARLY EXPLAIN THE MEANING OF THE GIVEN TEXT IN SIMPLE LANGUAGE.  
- IDENTIFY ANY AMBIGUITIES OR UNCLEAR PHRASES AND DISCUSS POSSIBLE INTERPRETATIONS.  
- CONCLUDE WITH A DEFINITIVE ANSWER BASED ON YOUR ANALYSIS.  

ENSURE THAT YOUR RESPONSE IS CONCISE, ACCURATE, AND ADHERES STRICTLY TO THE FORMATTING AND CONTENT REQUIREMENTS.  

IN ADDITION:  
- IDENTIFY NICHES AND DOMAIN-SPECIFIC FACTUAL INFORMATION THAT MAY BE USEFUL FOR FUTURE TASKS.  
- IF THE ASSISTANT HAS UTILIZED A GENERALIZABLE STRATEGY TO SOLVE A TASK, INCLUDE THAT STRATEGY IN THE INSTRUCTIONS.  
- ENSURE THAT THE RESPONSE IS ENCLOSED IN SQUARE BRACKETS FOR ALL WORDS.  
- INCLUDE SPECIFIC KEYWORDS AS REQUESTED IN THE INPUT, IF ANY.  
- IF THE TASK INVOLVES A CALCULATION, MAKE SURE TO USE THE APPROPRIATE FORMULA AND PROVIDE A CLEAR EXPLANATION.  
- IF THE TASK INVOLVES A TRANSLATION, MAKE SURE TO USE SIMPLE LANGUAGE AND AVOID ANY POTENTIAL AMBIGUITY.  
- IF THE TASK INVOLVES AN NLP TASK, MAKE SURE TO IDENTIFY THE KEY ELEMENTS AND THEIR RELATIONSHIP TO THE HYPOTHESIS.  
- IF THE TASK INVOLVES A LOGICAL INFERENCE, MAKE SURE TO EXPLAIN THE REASONING PROCESS AND PROVIDE A CLEAR CONCLUSION.  
- IF THE TASK INVOLVES A MATHEMATICAL PROBLEM, MAKE SURE TO PROVIDE A STEP-BY-STEP SOLUTION AND VERIFY THE ACCURACY OF THE FINAL ANSWER.  
- IF THE TASK INVOLVES A COMPLEX SYSTEM, MAKE SURE TO BREAK IT DOWN INTO SIMPLER COMPONENTS AND EXPLAIN EACH PART CLEARLY.  
- IF THE TASK INVOLVES A DATA ANALYSIS, MAKE SURE TO IDENTIFY THE RELEVANT DATA POINTS AND EXPLAIN HOW THEY RELATE TO THE QUESTION.  
- IF THE TASK INVOLVES A TECHNICAL PROBLEM, MAKE SURE TO PROVIDE A CLEAR EXPLANATION OF THE TECHNICAL TERMS AND THEIR MEANING.  
- IF THE TASK INVOLVES A REAL-WORLD SCENARIO, MAKE SURE TO RELATE THE SOLUTION BACK TO THE REAL-WORLD CONTEXT.  
- IF THE TASK INVOLVES A HYPOTHETICAL SITUATION, MAKE SURE TO EXPLAIN THE ASSUMPTIONS AND HOW THEY AFFECT THE OUTCOME.  
- IF THE TASK INVOLVES A COMPARATIVE ANALYSIS, MAKE SURE TO IDENTIFY THE KEY DIFFERENCES AND SIMILARITIES BETWEEN THE ELEMENTS BEING COMPARED.  
- IF THE TASK INVOLVES A TIME-BASED PROBLEM, MAKE SURE TO ACCOUNT FOR ALL TIME VARIABLES AND EXPLAIN HOW THEY AFFECT THE FINAL RESULT.  
- IF THE TASK INVOLVES A PROBABILITY OR STATISTICAL PROBLEM, MAKE SURE TO USE THE APPROPRIATE FORMULAS AND PROVIDE A CLEAR EXPLANATION OF THE CALCULATION PROCESS.

THE TASK INVOLVES SOLVING A PROBLEM RELATED TO THE MINIMUM NUMBER OF DECI-BINARY NUMBERS NEEDED TO SUM TO A GIVEN NUMBER. A DECI-BINARY NUMBER IS A NUMBER WHERE EACH DIGIT IS EITHER 0 OR 1 WITHOUT ANY LEADING ZEROS. THE GOAL IS TO DETERMINE THE MINIMUM NUMBER OF SUCH NUMBERS THAT SUM TO A GIVEN STRING REPRESENTING A POSITIVE INTEGER. THE SOLUTION IS BASED ON THE FACT THAT THE MINIMUM NUMBER OF DECI-BINARY NUMBERS REQUIRED IS EQUAL TO THE MAXIMUM DIGIT IN THE GIVEN NUMBER. THIS IS BECAUSE EACH DECI-BINARY NUMBER CAN CONTRIBUTE AT MOST 1 TO ANY DIGIT POSITION. THE SEQUENCE OF DECI-BINARY NUMBERS IS CONSTRUCTED BY PLACING 1S IN THE POSITIONS CORRESPONDING TO THE DIGITS OF THE INPUT NUMBER AND 0S ELSEWHERE. THE SOLUTION IS EFFICIENT, RUNNING IN LINEAR TIME RELATIVE TO THE LENGTH OF THE INPUT STRING. THIS APPROACH IS OPTIMAL AND SUITABLE FOR LARGE INPUTS AS SPECIFIED IN THE CONSTRAINTS.
